class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n<div id=\"text-block-5\" class=\"mk-text-block   page-intro\">\n\n\t\n\t<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #333333;\"><b>LEADERSHIP DEVELOPMENT DRIVES RESULTS.</b></span></h2>\n\n\t<div class=\"clearboth\"></div>\n</div>\n<div id=\"divider-6\" class=\"mk-divider custom-width center single_dotted \">\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"divider-inner\"></div>\n\t\n</div>\n<div class=\"clearboth\"></div>\n<div id=\"text-block-7\" class=\"mk-text-block   page-intro\">\n\n\t\n\t<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #00c4b4;\"><b>We Can Prove It.</b></span></h2>\n\n\t<div class=\"clearboth\"></div>\n</div>\n<div id=\"divider-8\" class=\"mk-divider custom-width center single_dotted \">\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"divider-inner\"></div>\n\t\n</div>\n<div class=\"clearboth\"></div></div></div></div>\t\t\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"wpb_row vc_inner vc_row    attched-false   vc_row-fluid\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n<div id=\"text-block-9\" class=\"mk-text-block   page-intro\">\n\n\t\n\t<p style=\"text-align: left;\">When it’s done right, leadership development transforms individuals, teams, organizations, and society. <strong>Leadership development is <em>all</em> we do – and we do it right.</strong> As our world-class rankings confirm, we also do it better than everyone else. Informed by decades of research and practical experience with tens of thousands of clients around the globe, our expertise drives measurable and enduring results.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">You know leadership really matters for solving your biggest challenges. That’s why your partner in leadership development matters, too. <a href=\"/articles/white-papers/driving-performance-how-leadership-development-powers-sustained-success/\">Learn what CCL can do for you</a>&nbsp;– and how we <a href=\"/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/proven-impact-the-power-of-leadership-development-done-right-center-for-creative-leadership.pdf\" target=\"_blank\">power change for our clients</a>.</p>\n\n\t<div class=\"clearboth\"></div>\n</div>\n</div></div></div>\t\t\n</div></div>\n\t</div>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wpb_row vc_row  mk-fullwidth-false  attched-false vc_custom_1476258726415  _ height-full\">\n\t</div>\n\n<div style=\"\" class=\"vc_col-sm-2 wpb_column column_container vc_custom_1476258747911  _ height-full\">\n\t\n\n<div class=\"wpb_row vc_inner vc_row   add-padding-0 attched-true   vc_row-fluid\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-6\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center  vc_custom_1484150703831\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"/transform-the-world/\" target=\"_self\"
